	@SuppressWarnings("deprecation")
	private NamespacedHierarchicalStore.CloseAction<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> createCloseAction() {
		return (__, ___, value) -> {
			boolean isAutoCloseEnabled = this.configuration.isClosingStoredAutoCloseablesEnabled();

			if (value instanceof @SuppressWarnings("resource") AutoCloseable closeable && isAutoCloseEnabled) {
				closeable.close();
				return;
			}

			if (value instanceof Store.CloseableResource resource) {
				if (isAutoCloseEnabled) {
					LOGGER.warn(
						() -> "Type implements CloseableResource but not AutoCloseable: " + value.getClass().getName());
				}
				resource.close();
			}
		};
	}

	private static NamespacedHierarchicalStore<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> createStore(
			@Nullable ExtensionContext parent, LauncherStoreFacade launcherStoreFacade,
			NamespacedHierarchicalStore.CloseAction<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> closeAction) {
		NamespacedHierarchicalStore<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> parentStore;
		if (parent == null) {
			parentStore = launcherStoreFacade.getRequestLevelStore();
		}
		else {
			parentStore = ((AbstractExtensionContext<?>) parent).valuesStore;
		}
		return new NamespacedHierarchicalStore<>(parentStore, closeAction);
	}

	@Override
	public void close() {
		this.valuesStore.close();
	}

		return getTestDescriptor().getUniqueId().toString();
	}

		return getTestDescriptor().getDisplayName();

	@SuppressWarnings("deprecation")
	private NamespacedHierarchicalStore.CloseAction<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> createCloseAction() {
		return (__, ___, value) -> {
			boolean isAutoCloseEnabled = this.configuration.isClosingStoredAutoCloseablesEnabled();

			if (value instanceof @SuppressWarnings("resource") AutoCloseable closeable && isAutoCloseEnabled) {
				closeable.close();
				return;
			}

			if (value instanceof Store.CloseableResource resource) {
				if (isAutoCloseEnabled) {
					Class<?> type = value.getClass();
					if (LOGGED_CLOSEABLE_RESOURCE_NOT_AUTOCLOSEABLE.add(type)) {
						LOGGER.warn(
							() -> "Type implements CloseableResource but not AutoCloseable: " + type.getName());
					}
				}
				resource.close();
			}
		};
	}

import org.junit.jupiter.engine.config.DefaultJupiterConfiguration;
import org.junit.platform.commons.logging.LoggerFactory;
import org.junit.platform.commons.logging.Logger;
import org.junit.platform.commons.JUnitException;
import org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.NamespacedHierarchicalStore;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.extension.ExtensionContext;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.extension.ExtensionContext.Store;

import java.lang.reflect.*;

public class reproduce_warning {
  static class MyResource implements Store.CloseableResource {
    @Override public void close() {}
  }

  public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
    // Create a minimal DefaultJupiterConfiguration with autoclose enabled
    DefaultJupiterConfiguration config = new DefaultJupiterConfiguration((key) -> null);

    // Reflectively create close action from AbstractExtensionContext by instantiating an anonymous subclass.
    Class<?> ctxClass = Class.forName("org.junit.jupiter.engine.descriptor.AbstractExtensionContext");

    // Find constructor
    Constructor<?> ctor = null;
    for (Constructor<?> c : ctxClass.getDeclaredConstructors()) {
      ctor = c;
      break;
    }
    if (ctor == null) throw new RuntimeException("No ctor");
    ctor.setAccessible(true);

    // We can't easily build all required args; instead directly invoke the static CloseAction logic by reflection:
    // call private createCloseAction() on a dummy instance created via Unsafe.
    Field theUnsafe = Class.forName("sun.misc.Unsafe").getDeclaredField("theUnsafe");
    theUnsafe.setAccessible(true);
    Object unsafe = theUnsafe.get(null);
    Method allocateInstance = unsafe.getClass().getMethod("allocateInstance", Class.class);
    Object ctx = allocateInstance.invoke(unsafe, ctxClass);

    // set configuration field
    Field cfgField = ctxClass.getDeclaredField("configuration");
    cfgField.setAccessible(true);
    cfgField.set(ctx, config);

    Method m = ctxClass.getDeclaredMethod("createCloseAction");
    m.setAccessible(true);
    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    NamespacedHierarchicalStore.CloseAction<?> action = (NamespacedHierarchicalStore.CloseAction<?>) m.invoke(ctx);

    Object val = new MyResource();
    for (int i=0;i<5;i++) {
      action.close(null,null,val);
    }
  }
}

+import org.junit.jupiter.engine.config.DefaultJupiterConfiguration;
+import org.junit.platform.commons.logging.LoggerFactory;
+import org.junit.platform.commons.logging.Logger;
+import org.junit.platform.commons.JUnitException;
+import org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.NamespacedHierarchicalStore;
+import org.junit.jupiter.api.extension.ExtensionContext;
+import org.junit.jupiter.api.extension.ExtensionContext.Store;
+
+import java.lang.reflect.*;
+
+public class reproduce_warning {
+  static class MyResource implements Store.CloseableResource {
+    @Override public void close() {}
+  }
+
+  public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
+    // Create a minimal DefaultJupiterConfiguration with autoclose enabled
+    DefaultJupiterConfiguration config = new DefaultJupiterConfiguration((key) -> null);
+
+    // Reflectively create close action from AbstractExtensionContext by instantiating an anonymous subclass.
+    Class<?> ctxClass = Class.forName("org.junit.jupiter.engine.descriptor.AbstractExtensionContext");
+
+    // Find constructor
+    Constructor<?> ctor = null;
+    for (Constructor<?> c : ctxClass.getDeclaredConstructors()) {
+      ctor = c;
+      break;
+    }
+    if (ctor == null) throw new RuntimeException("No ctor");
+    ctor.setAccessible(true);
+
+    // We can't easily build all required args; instead directly invoke the static CloseAction logic by reflection:
+    // call private createCloseAction() on a dummy instance created via Unsafe.
+    Field theUnsafe = Class.forName("sun.misc.Unsafe").getDeclaredField("theUnsafe");
+    theUnsafe.setAccessible(true);
+    Object unsafe = theUnsafe.get(null);
+    Method allocateInstance = unsafe.getClass().getMethod("allocateInstance", Class.class);
+    Object ctx = allocateInstance.invoke(unsafe, ctxClass);
+
+    // set configuration field
+    Field cfgField = ctxClass.getDeclaredField("configuration");
+    cfgField.setAccessible(true);
+    cfgField.set(ctx, config);
+
+    Method m = ctxClass.getDeclaredMethod("createCloseAction");
+    m.setAccessible(true);
+    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
+    NamespacedHierarchicalStore.CloseAction<?> action = (NamespacedHierarchicalStore.CloseAction<?>) m.invoke(ctx);
+
+    Object val = new MyResource();
+    for (int i=0;i<5;i++) {
+      action.close(null,null,val);
+    }
+  }
+}
